The staff here is SO supportive. I had my car towed here after hit-and-run accident and while they did not do the work because I had to eventually take it to an insurance collision place, they did a quick assessment to tell me it wasn't drivable for 120 miles (I was from out of town), kept me updated over the weekend. Very nice people: a big thanks to David and Mark.</review>

<Rating>5< /Rating><text>This is probably one of the larger Goodwill‚Äôs in the area. This is the time to get your Halloween costumes on the cheap! See the photos attached. A good portion in the center of the store was dedicated just to Halloween costumes.

More than half the store is clothes.
There is an entire other store right next to this one called OC Goodwill Boutique which is mostly high end, designer clothing with some couture. See my other review for those photos.

Not as much furniture at this Goodwill. Mostly side tables and chairs.
A good amount of housewares, small counter top appliances, lamps, home decor, linen, toys and shoes can be found here.

<user_id>112391776123966631195</user_id><user_name>Tim Harbage</user_name>< date>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Text>
The trails are nice for walking or biking, but the real gem is Tucker's Grove dog park (to the right and ALL the way down). It is a fantastic large fenced-in dog park. There are almost always other dogs there for your pup to play/socialize with. There is a water station, bags, balls, public bathrooms, and picnic tables/benches in the shade. It is well maintained, and there is even a coin operated dog wash station if your dog gets muddy. Good park and great dog park!<//Text>

<userid>113240326703452055174< /userid><user_name>Kelcie Moorman<//user_name><Time>1491508464740</Time>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
< Review>
This is a lovely, easy trail for a relaxing walk. The trail is mostly shaded by oaks and follows to the San Antonio creek. There are several creek crossings on the trail. The beginning of the path goes past the dog park, and continues on to end at highway 154. The whole trail took me a very leisurely hour one way. It probably could be done in 40-45 mins, so ~1.5 hrs total, if you're walking at a brisk pace. I took these photos on 4/5/16, and there are lots of beautiful wildflowers and green scenery. Gorgeous!!</Review>

<user>117605112696966034525</user>< name>
Gabriel Millos<//name>
< Date>
1548626270051</Date>
<Rating>5</Rating>< review>
A great little park to get away from civilization not far from Goleta or Santa Barbara. This is a county Park connected to Tucker's Grove Park (which closes at twilight every day). There is a dog park, some picnic areas, and a 1.5 mile trail that follows the creek up to the 154 (where there is another access point). The trail is usually well kept, not very strenuous, and very relaxing when the creek is flowing. Be careful of mountain bikers on the trail. Dogs should be kept on their leashes.  Please be sure to keep the park clean by not littering!< /review>

Has a great dog park with paths along the creek leading up to coffer dam. Pet washing station available, gopher holes with real gophers, fresh water station... dog heaven!  One improvement I would suggest is having a separate area for small dogs and/or timid dogs.  Sometimes the large dogs get a bit rowdy.  It would be nice to have a safe space for the small and timid dogs to escape to when needed.</review>

< Review>
A few months into the pandemic I recall wanting to write a review for markets for very similar reasons. My review pertains to my most recent visit. Working a customer facing job day in and day out can be different for every employee -- especially during a pandemic.

Digital Payment: Takes Samsung, not Apple, Pay. I don't know of other forms of digital payment.

Customer Service: Good though you may have to walk to the front to find an employee if the meat section isn't open or a knowledgeable employee isn't near you.

Products: Good selection, I mainly come here for a cereal discount/sale.

The store is usually clean. The aisles are big. The parking lot is huge.</Review>

<UserId.>109661421807561718444</UserId.><review>My husband and I shop at this Vons almost exclusively because of it's proximity to our home but also the selection and fair prices. I never thought to leave a review for a grocery store but tonight's visit warranted one. We initially stopped in for the basics but after mulling over what to eat for dinner, we decided to stop by the deli for some chicken. The young man working the deli tonight deserves some very high recognition. His name is Diland and I was beyond impressed with his customer service!

He helped us decide on the best deal for the chicken based on our discussion about quantity and let us know if we downloaded the Vons app, we could get the discount listed on the case (which was a solid $3+ off!). So we did. In the midst of sorting through the app details, he proceeded to bring a cart around to us and said "here you go, you need this more than I do!" He noticed that I was holding a few items in hand and my husband had an overflowing hand basket... not to mention I'm 8 months pregnant so holding anything other than a purse is quite the struggle.

I'm not sure why I was so blown away by his kindness, but I was. Having worked in many customer-facing jobs in the past, I know that sometimes it can get a little monotonous and frustrating to have to ALWAYS be nice, especially when you run into the occasional rude person. So I've felt that over the past few years, customer service has declined in all industries and customers have become more of a burden than someone employees are aiming to please. I have to say, Diland really went above and beyond to not only help us with a good deal, but to provide us with extra comfort that really isn't even part of his job! To say we were impressed is an understatement. He definitely deserves some recognition on here and by his management team. He's got some incredible personal skills that are sometimes hard to find in an employee.

Thank you Diland for putting a smile on our faces tonight :)< /review>< date>
